ALTER SESSION SET NLS_DATE_FORMAT = 'DD-MM-YYYY';

SET LINESIZE 250
SET PAGESIZE 900

/*
Lee Wee Yan (leader): table shelter, hospital, food_and_supply, hospital_admission (Checked by Tan Yong Yue)
Tan Yong Yue: table staff, disaster, disease, workload_allocation (Checked by Theng Chia Chia)
Theng Chia Chia: table victim, workload, donor, item_donation(Check by Lau Zhong Ren)
Lau Zhong Ren: table donation, body_examination, food_and_supply_allocation, shelter_allocation (Checked by Lee Wee Yan)
*/

DROP TABLE item_donation;
DROP TABLE shelter_allocation;
DROP TABLE hospital_admission;
DROP TABLE workload_allocation;
DROP TABLE body_examination;
DROP TABLE food_and_supply_allocation;
DROP TABLE donation;
DROP TABLE donor;
DROP TABLE disease;
DROP TABLE workload;
DROP TABLE disaster;
DROP TABLE food_and_supply;
DROP TABLE victim;
DROP TABLE staff;
DROP TABLE hospital;
DROP TABLE shelter;

Create table shelter(
    shelter_ID varchar(5) not null,
    shelter_name varchar(40) not null,
    shelter_capacity number(9) not null,
    street varchar(15) not null,
    city varchar(15) not null,
    state varchar(15) not null,
    email varchar(30) not null,
    contact varchar(12) not null,
primary key(shelter_ID) 
);

Create table hospital(
	hospital_ID varchar(5) not null, 
	hospital_name varchar(40) not null,
      street varchar(15) not null,
      city varchar(15) not null, 
	state varchar(15) not null, 
	email varchar(35) not null, 
	contact varchar(12) not null,
primary key(hospital_ID)
);

Create table staff(
	staff_ID varchar(5) not null,
	staff_name varchar(40)not null,
	gender char(1),
	date_of_birth date, 
	contact_number varchar(12) not null,
	email varchar(35)not null,
	position varchar(25) not null,
	salary number(7,2) DEFAULT 1000.00,
primary key(staff_ID),
constraint chk_gender check(UPPER(gender) IN ('M','F')),
constraint chk_email check(REGEXP_LIKE (email,'^[A-Za-z0-9.-_]\w+@(\S+)$'))
);

Create table victim(
	victim_ID varchar(5) not null,
	victim_name varchar(40) not null, 
	date_of_birth date, 
	gender char(1), 
	contact_number varchar(11) not null, 
	condition varchar(5) DEFAULT 'ALIVE', 
primary key(victim_ID),
constraint chk_gender2 check(UPPER(gender) IN ('M','F'))
);

Create table food_and_supply(
	food_supply_ID varchar(5) not null,
	item_name	varchar(25)not null,
	expired_date date,
	quantity_in_stock number(5) not null,
	description varchar(50),
primary key(food_supply_ID)
);

Create table disaster(
	disaster_ID varchar(5) not null, 
	disaster_type varchar(15) not null, 
	city_occur varchar(15), 
	date_occur date not null, 
primary key(disaster_ID)
);

Create table workload (
	workload_ID varchar(5) not null,
	workload_name varchar(40) not null,
	description varchar(65),
primary key(workload_ID)
);

Create table disease(
	disease_ID varchar(5) not null, 
	disease_name varchar(25) not null, 
	disease_symptom varchar(50), 
primary key(disease_ID)
);

Create table donor(
	donor_ID varchar(5) not null, 
	donor_name varchar(40) not null, 
	date_of_birth date, 
	gender char(1), 
	email varchar(35) not null,
primary key(donor_ID)
);

Create table donation(
	donation_ID  varchar(5) not null,
      donation_date date not null,
      cash_amount number(5), 
	donor_ID varchar(5),
primary key(donation_ID),
foreign key (donor_ID) references donor(donor_ID)
);

Create table food_and_supply_allocation(
	shelter_ID varchar(5) not null,
	food_supply_ID varchar(5) not null,
	allocation_date date,
	amount_allocated number(5) not null,
primary key(shelter_ID,food_supply_ID,amount_allocated),
foreign key (shelter_ID) references shelter(shelter_ID),
foreign key (food_supply_ID) references food_and_supply(food_supply_ID)
);

Create table body_examination(
	victim_ID varchar(5) not null,
	staff_ID varchar(5) not null,
	examination_date date not null,
	disease_ID varchar(5),
primary key(victim_ID,staff_ID,examination_date),
foreign key (victim_ID) references victim(victim_ID), 
foreign key (staff_ID) references staff(staff_ID),
foreign key (disease_ID) references disease(disease_ID)
);

Create table workload_allocation (
	staff_ID varchar(5) not null,
	workload_ID varchar(5) not null,
	working_date date not null,
	start_time char(5), 
	end_time char(5),
	shelter_ID varchar(5) not null,
primary key(staff_ID,workload_ID,working_date),
foreign key (staff_ID) references staff(staff_ID),
foreign key (workload_ID) references workload(workload_ID),
foreign key (shelter_ID) references  shelter(shelter_ID)
);


Create table hospital_admission(
	hospital_ID varchar(5) not null,
	victim_ID varchar(5) not null,
	admission_date date not null,
	discharge_date date not null, 
primary key(hospital_ID,victim_ID,admission_date),
foreign key (hospital_ID) references hospital(hospital_ID),
foreign key (victim_ID) references victim(victim_ID)
);


Create table shelter_allocation(
	shelter_ID varchar(5) not null,
	victim_ID varchar(5) not null,
	start_date date not null,
	end_date date not null,
	disaster_ID varchar(5) not null,
primary key(shelter_ID, victim_ID, start_date),
foreign key (shelter_ID) references shelter(shelter_ID),
foreign key (victim_ID) references victim(victim_ID)
);


Create table item_donation(
	food_supply_ID varchar(5) not null, 
	donation_ID varchar(5) not null, 
	quantity number(5) not null,
primary key(food_supply_ID,donation_ID),
foreign key (food_supply_ID) references food_and_supply(food_supply_ID),
foreign key (donation_ID) references donation(donation_ID)
);

FROM shelter;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Hospital
FROM hospital;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Staff
FROM staff;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Victim
FROM victim;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Food_And_Supply
FROM food_and_supply;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Disaster
FROM disaster;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Workload
FROM workload;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Disease
FROM disease;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Donor
FROM donor;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Donation
FROM donation;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_FoodAndSupplyAllocation
FROM food_and_supply_allocation;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Body_Examination
FROM body_examination;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Workload_Allocation
FROM workload_allocation;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Hospital_Admission
FROM hospital_admission;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Shelter_Allocation
FROM shelter_allocation;
SELECT COUNT(*) AS No_Of_Item_Donation
FROM item_donation;
